           <script>
            (function () {
  jQuery(window).on('user-object-created.adobe_target', function () {
    jQuery(window).off('user-object-created.adobe_target');
    window.targetPageParamsAll = function () {
      var tempUser = {};
      tempUser.user = {};
      tempUser.user.Raw = {};
      tempUser.user.Raw.adv_demographic = {};

      if (typeof User !== 'undefined' && User.hasOwnProperty('isLoggedIn')) {
        tempUser.user.isLoggedIn = User.isLoggedIn;
      }

      if (typeof User !== 'undefined' && User.hasOwnProperty('userID')) {
        tempUser.user.userId = User.userID;
      }

      if (typeof User !== 'undefined' && User.hasOwnProperty('user') && User.user.hasOwnProperty('Raw') && User.user.Raw.hasOwnProperty('addresses')) {
        if (User.user.Raw.addresses.length && typeof User.user.Raw.addresses[0] !== 'undefined' && User.user.Raw.addresses[0].hasOwnProperty('Shipping')) {
          tempUser.user.country = User.user.Raw.addresses[0].Shipping.country;
        }
      }

      if (typeof User !== 'undefined' && User.hasOwnProperty('user') && User.user.hasOwnProperty('Raw') && User.user.Raw.hasOwnProperty('adv_demographic')) {

        for (var _key in User.user.Raw.adv_demographic) {

          // Set the Advantage demographics
          if (/(_circStatus|_rate|_billStatus|_copies|_promoCode|_renewalFlag|_qualSrc|_donorType|_groupNumber)/.test(_key)) {
            tempUser.user.Raw.adv_demographic[_key] = User.user.Raw.adv_demographic[_key];
          }

          var prefix = _key.split('_')[0] || null;

          // Determine "expires in" keys
          if (User.user.Raw.adv_demographic.hasOwnProperty(_key) && /_finExp/.test(_key)) {
            var expVal = User.user.Raw.adv_demographic[_key];
            var _now = new Date();
            var _nowParsed = _now.getTime();
            var thirtyDaysFromNow = _now.setDate(_now.getDate() + 30);
            var ninetyDaysAgo = _now.setDate(_now.getDate() - 90);
            var expDate = Date.parse(expVal);
            
            tempUser.user[prefix + '_expiresWithin30Days'] = expDate < thirtyDaysFromNow && expDate > _nowParsed;
            tempUser.user[prefix + '_expiredWithinPast90Days'] = expDate > ninetyDaysAgo && expDate < _nowParsed;
          }

          // Determine the promo code exclusion custom variable
          if (User.user.Raw.adv_demographic.hasOwnProperty(_key) && /_promoCode/.test(_key)) {
            var _promoCode = User.user.Raw.adv_demographic[_key];
            tempUser.user[prefix + '_promoCodeExcluded'] = /^(D|G|H|S|Z)/.test(_promoCode);
          }

        }
      }

      return tempUser;
    };
    var adobeTargetParamsReady = new CustomEvent('adobeTargetParamsReady');
    document.querySelector('body').dispatchEvent(adobeTargetParamsReady);
  });
  if (typeof User !== 'undefined' && User.hasOwnProperty('user') && User.user !== null) {
    jQuery(window).trigger('user-object-created.adobe_target');
  }
})();

                       </div>

                          The automaker is cooperating with investigations that may also lead to fines or other sanctions by the U.S. Department of Justice or Securities and Exchange Commission, Bloomberg reported.

                        </a>

                  <div id="content_wrapper">
                   <form action="https://jobs.autonews.com/jobseeker/search/results/" class="jt_content" method="get" target="_blank">
                    <input name="site_id" type="hidden" value="2164"/>
                    <input class="search_bar" maxlength="200" name="t730" onblur="jt_onBlur(this)" onfocus="jt_onFocus(this)" type="text" value="Find Jobs"/>
                    <input class="primary-button search_submit" name="search_button" onclick="search_bar_value_jt_onClick();" type="button" value="go"/>
                   </form>
                   <div class="widgetlist">
                    <script charset="utf-8" language="javascript" src="https://jobs.autonews.com/distrib/jobs/javascript.cfm?code=YShR1brDZouZNPDYDYM3ceE5mwp7EPOj" target="_blank" type="text/javascript">
                    </script>

                 <script>
                  function jt_onBlur(el) {
    if (el.value == '') {
      el.value = el.defaultValue;
    }
  }
  function jt_onFocus(el) {
    if (el.value == el.defaultValue) {
      el.value = '';
    }
  }
  function search_bar_value_jt_onClick() {
    var valueSearch = document.getElementsByName('t730')[0].value;
    if (valueSearch == 'Find Jobs') {
      valueSearch = '';
    }
    window.open('https://jobs.autonews.com/jobseeker/search/?&site_id=2164&t730=' + valueSearch);
  }
                 </script>
